                <p>My parents were fated mates. That rare, sacred bond where two souls become one. Most wolves spend years yearning for that connection. Some fools reject it, seeing love as weakness. But my parents? Their bond forged them into legends. Together, they stood as Blackthorn Pack's most formidable protectors.</p>

                <p>Werewolves heal most wounds. But not this. Not when the mating bond shatters alongside your body. Most wolves follow their mates into death. My father stayed - broken, wheelchair-bound, a ghost of the warrior he'd been - just for me.</p>

                <p>He tries. He loves me. But that battle stole everything: his mate, his legs, his purpose. Some days, I wonder if death would've been kinder.</p>
